In response to (1), the management server designates this Envoy as a\n37:   //    healthchecker to health check a subset of all upstream hosts for a given\n38:   //    cluster (for example upstream Host 1 and Host 2). It streams\n39:   //    HealthCheckSpecifier messages with cluster related configuration for all\n40:   //    clusters this Envoy is designated to health check. {"type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01RkRSrahvwaJ1nzBeJBu3PA","type":"tool_result","content":"{\"content\":\"1: syntax = \\\"proto3\\\";\\n2: \\n3: package envoy.service.ext_proc.v3;\\n4: \\n5: import \\\"envoy/config/core/v3/base.proto\\\";\\n6: import \\\"envoy/extensions/filters/http/ext_proc/v3/processing_mode.proto\\\";\\n7: import \\\"envoy/type/v3/http_status.proto\\\";\\n8: \\n9: import \\\"google/protobuf/duration.proto\\\";\\n10: import \\\"google/protobuf/struct.proto\\\";\\n11: \\n12: import \\\"xds/annotations/v3/status.proto\\\";\\n13: \\n14: import \\\"envoy/annotations/deprecation.proto\\\";\\n15: import \\\"udpa/annotations/status.proto\\\";\\n16: import \\\"validate/validate.proto\\\";\\n17: \\n18: option java_package = \\\"io.envoyproxy.envoy.service.ext_proc.v3\\\";\\n19: option java_outer_classname = \\\"ExternalProcessorProto\\\";\\n20: option java_multiple_files = true;\\n21: option go_package = \\\"github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/service/ext_proc/v3;ext_procv3\\\";\\n22: option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;\\n23: \\n24: // [#protodoc-title: External processing service]\\n25: \\n26: // A service that can access and modify HTTP requests and responses as part of a filter chain.\\n27: // The overall external processing protocol works like this:\\n28: //\\n29: // 1. The data plane sends to the service information about the HTTP request.\\n30: // 2. The service sends back a ``ProcessingResponse`` message that directs the data plane to either\\n31: //    stop processing, continue without it, or send it the next chunk of the message body.\\n32: // 3. If so requested, the data plane sends the server the message body in chunks, or the entire\\n33: //    body at once. In either case, the server may send back a ``ProcessingResponse`` for each\\n34: //    message it receives, or wait for a certain amount of body chunks to be received before\\n35: //    streaming back the ``ProcessingResponse`` messages.\\n36: // 4. If so requested, the data plane sends the server the HTTP trailers, and the server sends back\\n37: //    a ``ProcessingResponse``.\\n38: // 5.
